# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  # Add to the front of the playList, ignore duplication #
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# The state of the playlist #
type PlayListState =
  + Playing(Id)
  + PausedOn(Id)
  + NoSongSelected
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the current state of the playlist #
type PlayList = ([Id], PlayListState) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_state: PlayList -> PlayListState =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, state = playlist in
    state
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =

    songs

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  # Add to the front of the playList, ignore duplication #
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# The state of the playlist #
type PlayListState =
  + Playing(Id)
  + PausedOn(Id)
  + NoSongSelected
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the current state of the playlist #
type PlayList = ([Id], PlayListState) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_state: PlayList -> PlayListState =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, state = playlist in
    state
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
    fun pl, action

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  # Add to the front of the playList, ignore duplication #
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# The state of the playlist #
type PlayListState =
  + Playing(Id)
  + PausedOn(Id)
  + NoSongSelected
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the current state of the playlist #
type PlayList = ([Id], PlayListState) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_state: PlayList -> PlayListState =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, state = playlist in
    state
in

let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
    fun pl, action ->

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  # Add to the front of the playList, ignore duplication #
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# The state of the playlist #
type PlayListState =
  + Playing(Id)
  + PausedOn(Id)
  + NoSongSelected
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the current state of the playlist #
type PlayList = ([Id], PlayListState) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_state: PlayList -> PlayListState =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, state = playlist in
    state
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
    fun pl, action ->
      case action

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  # Add to the front of the playList, ignore duplication #
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# The state of the playlist #
type PlayListState =
  + Playing(Id)
  + PausedOn(Id)
  + NoSongSelected
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the current state of the playlist #
type PlayList = ([Id], PlayListState) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_state: PlayList -> PlayListState =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, state = playlist in
    state
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
    fun pl, action ->
      case action

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  # Add to the front of the playList, ignore duplication #
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# The state of the playlist #
type PlayListState =
  + Playing(Id)
  + PausedOn(Id)
  + NoSongSelected
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the current state of the playlist #
type PlayList = ([Id], PlayListState) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_state: PlayList -> PlayListState =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, state = playlist in
    state
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
    fun pl, action ->
      case action 
        | Play

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  # Add to the front of the playList, ignore duplication #
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# The state of the playlist #
type PlayListState =
  + Playing(Id)
  + PausedOn(Id)
  + NoSongSelected
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the current state of the playlist #
type PlayList = ([Id], PlayListState) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_state: PlayList -> PlayListState =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, state = playlist in
    state
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
    fun pl, action ->
      case action 
        | PlaySong(

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  # Add to the front of the playList, ignore duplication #
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# The state of the playlist #
type PlayListState =
  + Playing(Id)
  + PausedOn(Id)
  + NoSongSelected
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the current state of the playlist #
type PlayList = ([Id], PlayListState) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_state: PlayList -> PlayListState =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, state = playlist in
    state
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
    fun pl, action ->
      case action 
        | PlaySong(id) =>
            max_

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  # Add to the front of the playList, ignore duplication #
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# The state of the playlist #
type PlayListState =
  + Playing(Id)
  + PausedOn(Id)
  + NoSongSelected
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the current state of the playlist #
type PlayList = ([Id], PlayListState) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_state: PlayList -> PlayListState =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, state = playlist in
    state
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
    fun pl, action ->
      case action 
        | PlaySong(id) =>
            max_int ::

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  # Add to the front of the playList, ignore duplication #
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# The state of the playlist #
type PlayListState =
  + Playing(Id)
  + PausedOn(Id)
  + NoSongSelected
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the current state of the playlist #
type PlayList = ([Id], PlayListState) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_state: PlayList -> PlayListState =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, state = playlist in
    state
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
    fun pl, action ->
      case action 
        | PlaySong(id) =>
            max_int ::

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  # Add to the front of the playList, ignore duplication #
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# The state of the playlist #
type PlayListState =
  + Playing(Id)
  + PausedOn(Id)
  + NoSongSelected
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the current state of the playlist #
type PlayList = ([Id], PlayListState) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_state: PlayList -> PlayListState =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, state = playlist in
    state
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
    fun pl, action ->
      case action 
        | PlaySong(id) =>
            max_int :: 1 + 2

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  # Add to the front of the playList, ignore duplication #
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# The state of the playlist #
type PlayListState =
  + Playing(Id)
  + PausedOn(Id)
  + NoSongSelected
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the current state of the playlist #
type PlayList = ([Id], PlayListState) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_state: PlayList -> PlayListState =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, state = playlist in
    state
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
    fun pl, action ->
      case action 
        | PlaySong(id) =>
            max_int :: 1 + 2
          end

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  # Add to the front of the playList, ignore duplication #
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# The state of the playlist #
type PlayListState =
  + Playing(Id)
  + PausedOn(Id)
  + NoSongSelected
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the current state of the playlist #
type PlayList = ([Id], PlayListState) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_state: PlayList -> PlayListState =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, state = playlist in
    state
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
    fun pl, action ->
      case action 
        | PlaySong(id) =>
            max_int :: 1 + 2
          end in

  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  # Add to the front of the playList, ignore duplication #
  + AddSong(Id)

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  # Add to the front of the playList, ignore duplication #
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# The state of the playlist #
type PlayListState =
  + Playing(Id)
  + PausedOn(Id)
  + NoSongSelected
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the current state of the playlist #
type PlayList = ([Id], PlayListState) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_state: PlayList -> PlayListState =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, state = playlist in
    state
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
    fun pl, action ->
      case action 
        | PlaySong(id) =>
            max_int :: 1 + 2
          end in
          case par

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  # Add to the front of the playList, ignore duplication #
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# The state of the playlist #
type PlayListState =
  + Playing(Id)
  + PausedOn(Id)
  + NoSongSelected
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the current state of the playlist #
type PlayList = ([Id], PlayListState) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_state: PlayList -> PlayListState =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, state = playlist in
    state
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
    fun pl, action ->
      case action 
        | PlaySong(id) =>
            max_int :: 1 + 2
          end in
          case parse_

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  # Add to the front of the playList, ignore duplication #
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# The state of the playlist #
type PlayListState =
  + Playing(Id)
  + PausedOn(Id)
  + NoSongSelected
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the current state of the playlist #
type PlayList = ([Id], PlayListState) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_state: PlayList -> PlayListState =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, state = playlist in
    state
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
    fun pl, action ->
      case action 
        | PlaySong(id) =>

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  # Add to the front of the playList, ignore duplication #
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# The state of the playlist #
type PlayListState =
  + Playing(Id)
  + PausedOn(Id)
  + NoSongSelected
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the current state of the playlist #
type PlayList = ([Id], PlayListState) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_state: PlayList -> PlayListState =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, state = playlist in
    state
in

type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  # Add to the front of the playList, ignore duplication #
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# The state of the playlist #
type PlayListState =
  + Playing(Id)
  + PausedOn(Id)
  + NoSongSelected
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the current state of the playlist #
type PlayList = ([Id], PlayListState) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_state: PlayList -> PlayListState =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, state = playlist in
    state
in

            max_int :: 1 + 2

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  # Add to the front of the playList, ignore duplication #
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# The state of the playlist #
type PlayListState =
  + Playing(Id)
  + PausedOn(Id)
  + NoSongSelected
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the current state of the playlist #
type PlayList = ([Id], PlayListState) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_state: PlayList -> PlayListState =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, state = playlist in
    state
in

    fun pl, action ->
      case action 
        | PlaySong(id) =>
            max_int :: 1 + 2

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  # Add to the front of the playList, ignore duplication #
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# The state of the playlist #
type PlayListState =
  + Playing(Id)
  + PausedOn(Id)
  + NoSongSelected
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the current state of the playlist #
type PlayList = ([Id], PlayListState) in

  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  # Add to the front of the playList, ignore duplication #
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# The state of the playlist #
type PlayListState =
  + Playing(Id)
  + PausedOn(Id)
  + NoSongSelected
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the current state of the playlist #
type PlayList = ([Id], PlayListState) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_state: PlayList -> PlayListState =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, state = playlist in
    state
in

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  # Add to the front of the playList, ignore duplication #
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# The state of the playlist #
type PlayListState =
  + Playing(Id)
  + PausedOn(Id)
  + NoSongSelected
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the current state of the playlist #
type PlayList = ([Id], PlayListState) in

  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  # Add to the front of the playList, ignore duplication #
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# The state of the playlist #
type PlayListState =
  + Playing(Id)
  + PausedOn(Id)
  + NoSongSelected
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the current state of the playlist #
type PlayList = ([Id], PlayListState) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

  fun playlist ->
    let songs, state = playlist in
    state
in

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  # Add to the front of the playList, ignore duplication #
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# The state of the playlist #
type PlayListState =
  + Playing(Id)
  + PausedOn(Id)
  + NoSongSelected
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the current state of the playlist #
type PlayList = ([Id], PlayListState) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_state: PlayList -> PlayListState =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, state = playlist in
    state
in

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  # Add to the front of the playList, ignore duplication #
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# The state of the playlist #
type PlayListState =
  + Playing(Id)
  + PausedOn(Id)
  + NoSongSelected
in

  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

    state

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  # Add to the front of the playList, ignore duplication #
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# The state of the playlist #
type PlayListState =
  + Playing(Id)
  + PausedOn(Id)
  + NoSongSelected
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the current state of the playlist #
type PlayList = ([Id], PlayListState) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_state: PlayList -> PlayListState =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, state = playlist in
    state
in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  # Add to the front of the playList, ignore duplication #
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# The state of the playlist #
type PlayListState =
  + Playing(Id)
  + PausedOn(Id)
  + NoSongSelected
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the current state of the playlist #
type PlayList = ([Id], PlayListState) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_state: PlayList -> PlayListState =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, state = playlist in
    state
in

    fun pl, action ->
      case action 
        | PlaySong(id) =>
            max_int :: 1 + 2
